js/ui/pages/RehabPage.js
```
// js/ui/pages/RehabPage.js
// Обновлённая версия — читает данные из Context

import React, { useContext } from 'react';
import { AppStateContext, AppDispatchContext } from '../../core/AppContext.js';
import { MORNING_ROUTINE, EVENING_ROUTINE } from '../../config/constants.js';

function RoutineList({ title, routines, done, onMarkDone, icon }) {
  const items = routines.map((item, i) =>
    React.createElement(
      'div',
      { key: i, className: 'routine-item' },
      React.createElement(
        'div',
        { style: { flex: 1 } },
        React.createElement('div', { style: { fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '0.9rem' } }, item.name),
        React.createElement(
          'div',
          { className: 'text-sm', style: { color: 'var(--text2)', marginTop: '0.125rem' } },
          `${item.reps} — ${item.why}`
        )
      )
    )
  );

  return React.createElement(
    'div',
    { className: 'card' },
    React.createElement(
      'div',
      { style: { display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', marginBottom: '0.75rem' } },
      React.createElement('h3', { style: { margin: 0, fontSize: '1.05rem' } }, `${icon} ${title}`),
      React.createElement(
        'button',
        { className: done ? 'btn btn-sm btn-green' : 'btn btn-sm btn-accent', onClick: onMarkDone },
        done ? '✓ Выполнено' : 'Отметить'
      )
    ),
    items
  );
}

export default function RehabPage() {
  const state = useContext(AppStateContext);
  const dispatch = useContext(AppDispatchContext);

  const { morningDone, eveningDone } = state;
  const { handleMarkMorning, handleMarkEvening } = dispatch;

  return React.createElement(
    'div',
    { className: 'page-enter' },
    React.createElement('h2', null, 'Реабилитация'),
    React.createElement(
      'p',
      { className: 'text-sm', style: { color: 'var(--text2)', marginBottom: '1rem' } },
      'Ежедневные рутины для поддержания здоровья суставов и дыхательной системы'
    ),
    React.createElement(RoutineList, {
      title: 'Утренняя активация',
      routines: MORNING_ROUTINE,
      done: morningDone,
      onMarkDone: handleMarkMorning,
      icon: '☀️',
    }),
    React.createElement(RoutineList, {
      title: 'Вечернее расслабление',
      routines: EVENING_ROUTINE,
      done: eveningDone,
      onMarkDone: handleMarkEvening,
      icon: '🌙',
    })
  );
}
```

Теперь нужно обновить `app.js` — RehabPage больше не принимает props, а читает из Context. Также нужно убедиться, что `SessionPlan`, `CoachAdvice`, `QuickStats` существуют как компоненты. Поскольку они используются в `TodayPage.js`, но их файлы не были предоставлены, я создам минимальные заглушки для них, чтобы приложение не ломалось. Также нужно проверить `LogPage.js` — он ссылается на `CheckinForm` и `SessionLogger`.

Давайте создам недостающие компоненты-заглушки и обновлю `app.js`:

js/ui/pages/SessionPlan.js
```
// js/ui/pages/SessionPlan.js
// План тренировки — отображает упражнения из sessionPlan

import React from 'react';

export default function SessionPlan({ sessionPlan, trainType, weekLabel, apreReasons }) {
  if (!sessionPlan) return null;

  const exercises = sessionPlan.exercises || [];

  const exerciseElements = exercises.map((ex, i) =>
    React.createElement(
      'div',
      { key: i, className: `exercise ${ex.isTest ? 'exercise-test' : ''}` },
      React.createElement('div', { className: 'exercise-name' }, ex.n),
      React.createElement('div', { className: 'exercise-detail' },
        `${ex.s} подходов × ${ex.r}`
      ),
      ex.w && React.createElement('div', { className: 'exercise-note' }, ex.w)
    )
  );

  return React.createElement(
    React.Fragment,
    null,
    React.createElement(
      'div',
      { className: 'card card-elevated' },
      React.createElement(
        'div',
        { style: { display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', marginBottom: '0.75rem' } },
        React.createElement('h3', { style: { margin: 0, fontSize: '1.05rem' } }, sessionPlan.label || trainType),
        React.createElement('span', { className: `pill ${sessionPlan.mode === 'full' ? 'green' : sessionPlan.mode === 'yellow' ? 'yellow' : 'red'}` },
          { full: 'Полный', yellow: 'Облегчённый', minimum: 'Минимальный' }[sessionPlan.mode] || sessionPlan.mode
        )
      ),
      weekLabel && React.createElement('div', { style: { fontSize: '0.8rem', color: 'var(--text2)', marginBottom: '0.5rem' } }, weekLabel),
      exerciseElements
    ),
    apreReasons && apreReasons.length > 0 && React.createElement(
      'div',
      { className: 'apre-card' },
      React.createElement('h4', null, 'Авторегуляция'),
      apreReasons.map((r, i) =>
        React.createElement('div', { key: i, className: 'apre-item' }, r)
      )
    )
  );
}

js/ui/pages/CoachAdvice.js
```
// js/ui/pages/CoachAdvice.js
// Советы тренера на основе Recovery Score и метрик

import React from 'react';

export default function CoachAdvice({ advice }) {
  if (!advice || advice.length === 0) return null;

  return React.createElement(
    'div',
    { className: 'coach-advice-card' },
    React.createElement('h4', null, 'Советы тренера'),
    advice.map((tip, i) =>
      React.createElement('div', { key: i, className: 'coach-advice-item' }, tip)
    )
  );

// js/ui/pages/QuickStats.js
// Быстрая статистика: завтра + утренняя/вечерняя рутины

import React from 'react';

export default function QuickStats({ tomorrowType, tomorrowPlan, morningDone, eveningDone, onMarkMorning, onMarkEvening }) {
  return React.createElement(
    React.Fragment,
    null,
    // Tomorrow preview
    tomorrowType && tomorrowPlan && React.createElement(
      'div',
      { className: 'card' },
      React.createElement('h4', { style: { margin: '0 0 0.5rem 0', fontSize: '0.85rem', color: 'var(--text2)', textTransform: 'uppercase', letterSpacing: '0.03em' } }, 'Завтра'),
      React.createElement(
        'div',
        { className: 'tomorrow-preview' },
        React.createElement('span', { className: 'tomorrow-preview-label' }, tomorrowPlan.label || tomorrowType),
        React.createElement('span', { className: 'tomorrow-preview-value' },
          `${(tomorrowPlan.exercises || []).length} упражнений`
        )
      )
    ),
    // Morning / Evening routines
    React.createElement(
      'div',
      { className: 'card' },
      React.createElement('h4', { style: { margin: '0 0 0.75rem 0', fontSize: '0.85rem', color: 'var(--text2)', textTransform: 'uppercase', letterSpacing: '0.03em' } }, 'Рутины'),
      React.createElement(
        'div',
        { style: { display: 'flex', gap: '0.5rem' } },
        React.createElement(
          'button',
          {
            className: morningDone ? 'btn btn-sm btn-green' : 'btn btn-sm btn-outline',
            onClick: onMarkMorning,
            style: { flex: 1 },
          },
          morningDone ? '☀️ Утро ✓' : '☀️ Утро'
        ),
        React.createElement(
          'button',
          {
            className: eveningDone ? 'btn btn-sm btn-green' : 'btn btn-sm btn-outline',
            onClick: onMarkEvening,
            style: { flex: 1 },
          },
          eveningDone ? '🌙 Вечер ✓' : '🌙 Вечер'
        )
      )
    )
  );
}

// Форма ежедневного чек-ина

import React, { useContext } from 'react';
import { AppStateContext, AppDispatchContext } from '../../core/AppContext.js';

export default function CheckinForm() {
  const state = useContext(AppStateContext);
  const dispatch = useContext(AppDispatchContext);

  const {
    weight, restHR, hrv, sleepHours, hipPain, shoulderPain, breathing, notes,
    muscleSoreness, energy, mood, sleepQuality, stress, readiness,
  } = state;

  const {
    setWeight, setRestHR, setHrv, setSleepHours,
    setHipPain, setShoulderPain, setBreathing, setNotes,
    setMuscleSoreness, setEnergy, setMood, setSleepQuality, setStress,
    handleSaveCheckin,
  } = dispatch;

  const inputStyle = { width: '100%', boxSizing: 'border-box' };
  const labelStyle = { fontSize: '0.85rem', fontWeight: 500, display: 'block', marginBottom: '0.25rem' };

      'div',

        'div',
        { style: { display: 'flex', gap: '0.25rem' } },

            key: n,

            onClick: () => setter(n),

      )
    );

js\ui\pages\RehabPage.js
```
import React from 'react';
import { MORNING_ROUTINE, EVENING_ROUTINE } from '../../config/constants.js';

function RoutineList({ title, routines, done, onMarkDone, color, icon }) {
  const items = routines.map((item, i) =>
    React.createElement(
      'div',
      {
        key: i,
        className: 'routine-item',
      },
      React.createElement(
        'div',
        { style: { flex: 1 } },
        React.createElement(
          'div',
          { style: { fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '0.9rem' } },
          item.name
        ),
        React.createElement(
          'div',
          { className: 'text-sm', style: { color: 'var(--text2)', marginTop: '0.125rem' } },
          `${item.reps} — ${item.why}`
        )
      )
    )
  );

  return React.createElement(
    'div',
    { className: 'card' },
    React.createElement(
      'div',
      {
        style: {
          display: 'flex',
          justifyContent: 'space-between',
          alignItems: 'center',
          marginBottom: '0.75rem',
        }
      },
      React.createElement('h3', { style: { margin: 0, fontSize: '1.05rem' } }, `${icon} ${title}`),
      React.createElement(
        'button',
        {
          className: done ? 'btn btn-sm btn-green' : 'btn btn-sm btn-accent',
          onClick: onMarkDone,
        },
        done ? '\u2713 Выполнено' : 'Отметить'
      )
    ),
    items
  );
}

export default function RehabPage({ morningDone, eveningDone, markMorning, markEvening }) {
  return React.createElement(
    'div',
    { className: 'page-enter' },
    React.createElement('h2', null, 'Реабилитация'),
    React.createElement(
      'p',
      { className: 'text-sm', style: { color: 'var(--text2)', marginBottom: '1rem' } },
      'Ежедневные рутины для поддержания здоровья суставов и дыхательной системы'
    ),
    React.createElement(RoutineList, {
      title: 'Утренняя активация',
      routines: MORNING_ROUTINE,
      done: morningDone,
      onMarkDone: markMorning,
      icon: '\u2600\uFE0F',
    }),
    React.createElement(RoutineList, {
      title: 'Вечернее расслабление',
      routines: EVENING_ROUTINE,
      done: eveningDone,
      onMarkDone: markEvening,
      icon: '\uD83C\uDF19',
    })
  );
}

js/ui/components/ReadinessRing.js
```
import React, { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';

const RING_SIZE = 180;
const STROKE = 10;
const RADIUS = (RING_SIZE - STROKE) / 2;
const CIRCUMFERENCE = 2 * Math.PI * RADIUS;

function readinessColor(readiness) {
  if (readiness === 'green') return 'var(--green)';
  if (readiness === 'yellow') return 'var(--yellow)';
  if (readiness === 'red') return 'var(--red)';
  return 'var(--surface3)';
}

function readinessLabel(readiness) {
  if (readiness === 'green') return 'Готов';
  if (readiness === 'yellow') return 'Средне';
  if (readiness === 'red') return 'Отдых';
  return '—';
}

function scoreColor(score) {
  if (score >= 70) return 'var(--green)';
  if (score >= 40) return 'var(--yellow)';
  return 'var(--red)';
}

export default function ReadinessRing({ readiness, autoReadiness, manualOverride, onManualOverrideChange, recoveryScore }) {
  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false);
  const [animProgress, setAnimProgress] = useState(0);
  const animRef = useRef(null);

  const effectiveReadiness = manualOverride || autoReadiness || readiness;
  const color = readinessColor(effectiveReadiness);
  const label = readinessLabel(effectiveReadiness);
  const score = typeof recoveryScore === 'number' ? Math.round(recoveryScore) : null;

  useEffect(() => {
    let start = null;
    const duration = 800;
    const animate = (ts) => {
      if (!start) start = ts;
      const elapsed = ts - start;
      const progress = Math.min(elapsed / duration, 1);
      // ease-out cubic
      const eased = 1 - Math.pow(1 - progress, 3);
      setAnimProgress(eased);
      if (progress < 1) {
        animRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
      }
    };
    animRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    return () => { if (animRef.current) cancelAnimationFrame(animRef.current); };
  }, [readiness, recoveryScore]);

  const offset = CIRCUMFERENCE - (CIRCUMFERENCE * (score || 0) / 100) * animProgress;

  return React.createElement(
    'div',
    { className: 'hero-ring-container' },
    React.createElement(
      'div',
      {
        className: 'hero-ring',
        onClick: () => setExpanded(e => !e),
        role: 'button',
        tabIndex: 0,
        'aria-label': `Recovery score ${score}, readiness ${label}`,
        onKeyDown: (e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') setExpanded(prev => !prev); },
      },
      React.createElement(
        'svg',
        { width: RING_SIZE, height: RING_SIZE, className: 'hero-ring-svg', viewBox: `0 0 ${RING_SIZE} ${RING_SIZE}` },
        // Background circle
        React.createElement('circle', {
          cx: RING_SIZE / 2,
          cy: RING_SIZE / 2,
          r: RADIUS,
          className: 'hero-ring-bg',
        }),
        // Foreground arc
        React.createElement('circle', {
          cx: RING_SIZE / 2,
          cy: RING_SIZE / 2,
          r: RADIUS,
          fill: 'none',
          stroke: color,
          strokeWidth: STROKE,
          strokeLinecap: 'round',
          strokeDasharray: CIRCUMFERENCE,
          strokeDashoffset: offset,
          className: 'hero-ring-fg',
          style: { transition: 'stroke-dashoffset 0.1s ease-out' },
        }),
        // Score text
        React.createElement(
          'text',
          {
            x: RING_SIZE / 2,
            y: RING_SIZE / 2 - 6,
            textAnchor: 'middle',
            className: 'hero-ring-score',
            fill: scoreColor(score),
            style: { fontSize: '2.8rem', fontWeight: 800, fontFamily: 'var(--font-mono)' },
          },
          score !== null ? String(score) : '—'
        ),
        // Label text
        React.createElement(
          'text',
          {
            x: RING_SIZE / 2,
            y: RING_SIZE / 2 + 18,
            textAnchor: 'middle',
            className: 'hero-ring-label-text',
            fill: 'var(--text2)',
            style: { fontSize: '0.72rem', fontWeight: 500 },
          },
          'Восстановление'
        )
      ),
      // Readiness badge below ring
      React.createElement(
        'div',
        { className: 'hero-readiness-badge' },
        React.createElement('span', { className: `pill pill-solid ${effectiveReadiness || 'gray'}` }, label)
      ),
      // Tap hint
      React.createElement(
        'div',
        { className: 'hero-ring-hint' },
        expanded ? 'Свернуть' : 'Тап для трендов'
      )
    ),
    // Manual override (small, below)
    onManualOverrideChange &&
      React.createElement(
        'div',
        { className: 'hero-manual-override' },
        React.createElement(
          'label',
          { className: 'text-xs', style: { color: 'var(--text3)', marginRight: '0.5rem' } },
          'Вручную:'
        ),
        React.createElement(
          'select',
          {
            value: manualOverride || '',
            onChange: e => onManualOverrideChange(e.target.value || null),
            className: 'hero-override-select',
          },
          React.createElement('option', { value: '' }, 'Авто'),
          React.createElement('option', { value: 'green' }, 'Зелёный'),
          React.createElement('option', { value: 'yellow' }, 'Жёлтый'),
          React.createElement('option', { value: 'red' }, 'Красный'),
        )
      )
  );
}
```

js/ui/components/RecoveryBar.js
```
import React, { useRef, useEffect, useState } from 'react';

function barColor(score) {
  if (score >= 70) return 'var(--green)';
  if (score >= 40) return 'var(--yellow)';
  return 'var(--red)';
}

export default function RecoveryBar({ score }) {
  const [width, setWidth] = useState(0);
  const animRef = useRef(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    let start = null;
    const duration = 600;
    const target = typeof score === 'number' ? Math.min(Math.max(score, 0), 100) : 0;
    const animate = (ts) => {
      if (!start) start = ts;
      const elapsed = ts - start;
      const progress = Math.min(elapsed / duration, 1);
      const eased = 1 - Math.pow(1 - progress, 3);
      setWidth(target * eased);
      if (progress < 1) {
        animRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
      }
    };
    animRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    return () => { if (animRef.current) cancelAnimationFrame(animRef.current); };
  }, [score]);

  return React.createElement(
    'div',
    { className: 'recovery-bar-wrapper' },
    React.createElement(
      'div',
      { className: 'recovery-bar-labels' },
      React.createElement('span', { className: 'text-xs', style: { color: 'var(--text2)' } }, 'Восстановление'),
      React.createElement(
        'span',
        {
          className: 'text-xs',
          style: { color: barColor(score), fontWeight: 700, fontFamily: 'var(--font-mono)' },
        },
        typeof score === 'number' ? `${Math.round(score)}%` : '—'
      )
    ),
    React.createElement(
      'div',
      { className: 'recovery-bar' },
      React.createElement('div', {
        className: 'recovery-bar-fill',
        style: {
          width: `${width}%`,
          backgroundColor: barColor(score),
        },
      })
    )
  );
}
```

js/ui/components/ExerciseCard.js
```
import React, { useState } from 'react';

function trainTypeLabel(type) {
  if (type === 'A') return 'Тяга';
  if (type === 'B') return 'Жим';
  if (type === 'C') return 'Всё тело';
  return type || '—';
}

function trainTypeIcon(type) {
  if (type === 'A') return '🏋️';
  if (type === 'B') return '💪';
  if (type === 'C') return '🔥';
  return '🏃';
}

export default function ExerciseCard({ sessionPlan, trainType, weekLabel, apreReasons }) {
  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false);

  if (!sessionPlan) {
    return React.createElement(
      'div',
      { className: 'card exercise-card' },
      React.createElement(
        'div',
        { className: 'exercise-card-header' },
        React.createElement('span', { className: 'exercise-card-icon' }, '😴'),
        React.createElement('h3', { className: 'exercise-card-title' }, 'День отдыха'),
      ),
      React.createElement(
        'p',
        { className: 'text-sm', style: { color: 'var(--text2)' } },
        'Сегодня восстановление. Сделай утреннюю рутину и лёгкую прогулку.'
      )
    );
  }

  const exercises = sessionPlan.exercises || [];
  const isTestDay = sessionPlan.isTestDay;

  return React.createElement(
    'div',
    { className: `card exercise-card ${isTestDay ? 'exercise-card-test' : ''}` },
    // Header
    React.createElement(
      'div',
      { className: 'exercise-card-header' },
      React.createElement('span', { className: 'exercise-card-icon' }, trainTypeIcon(trainType)),
      React.createElement(
        'div',
        { className: 'exercise-card-info' },
        React.createElement(
          'h3',
          { className: 'exercise-card-title' },
          `${trainTypeLabel(trainType)} ${weekLabel ? `· ${weekLabel}` : ''}`
        ),
        React.createElement(
          'span',
          { className: 'text-xs', style: { color: 'var(--text3)' } },
          `${exercises.length} упражнений${isTestDay ? ' · Тестовый день' : ''}`
        )
      ),
      React.createElement(
        'button',
        {
          className: 'btn btn-sm btn-outline exercise-card-toggle',
          onClick: () => setExpanded(e => !e),
          'aria-expanded': expanded,
        },
        expanded ? 'Свернуть' : 'Подробнее'
      )
    ),

    // APRE reasons (always visible, compact)
    apreReasons && apreReasons.length > 0 &&
      React.createElement(
        'div',
        { className: 'exercise-apre-badges' },
        apreReasons.map((r, i) =>
          React.createElement('span', { key: i, className: 'pill pill yellow', style: { fontSize: '0.7rem' } }, r)
        )
      ),

    // Expanded exercise list
    expanded &&
      React.createElement(
        'div',
        { className: 'exercise-list' },
        exercises.map((ex, i) =>
          React.createElement(
            'div',
            { key: i, className: `exercise-item ${ex.isTest ? 'exercise-item-test' : ''}` },
            React.createElement(
              'div',
              { className: 'exercise-item-main' },
              React.createElement('span', { className: 'exercise-item-name' }, ex.name),
              React.createElement(
                'span',
                { className: 'exercise-item-detail' },
                ex.isTest ? 'Максимум' : `${ex.sets}×${ex.reps}`
              )
            ),
            ex.note &&
              React.createElement('span', { className: 'exercise-item-note' }, ex.note)
          )
        )
      )
  );
}
```

js/ui/components/TomorrowPreview.js
```
import React from 'react';

function trainTypeLabel(type) {
  if (type === 'A') return 'Тяга';
  if (type === 'B') return 'Жим';
  if (type === 'C') return 'Всё тело';
  if (!type) return 'Отдых';
  return type;
}

function trainTypeIcon(type) {
  if (type === 'A') return '🏋️';
  if (type === 'B') return '💪';
  if (type === 'C') return '🔥';
  return '😴';
}

export default function TomorrowPreview({
  tomorrowType, tomorrowPlan,
  morningDone, eveningDone,
  onMarkMorning, onMarkEvening,
}) {
  return React.createElement(
    React.Fragment,
    null,
    // Tomorrow preview
    React.createElement(
      'div',
      { className: 'card tomorrow-card' },
      React.createElement(
        'div',
        { className: 'tomorrow-card-inner' },
        React.createElement('span', { className: 'tomorrow-icon' }, trainTypeIcon(tomorrowType)),
        React.createElement(
          'div',
          null,
          React.createElement('div', { className: 'tomorrow-label' }, 'Завтра'),
          React.createElement(
            'div',
            { className: 'tomorrow-value' },
            tomorrowType ? `${trainTypeLabel(tomorrowType)} · ${(tomorrowPlan && tomorrowPlan.exercises || []).length} упр.` : 'День отдыха'
          )
        )
      )
    ),

    // Morning / Evening routines
    React.createElement(
      'div',
      { className: 'card routine-card' },
      React.createElement('h4', { className: 'routine-card-title' }, 'Ежедневные рутины'),
      React.createElement(
        'div',
        { className: 'routine-buttons' },
        React.createElement(
          'button',
          {
            className: `btn btn-sm routine-btn ${morningDone ? 'btn-green' : 'btn-outline'}`,
            onClick: onMarkMorning,
          },
          morningDone ? '☀️ Утро ✓' : '☀️ Утро'
        ),
        React.createElement(
          'button',
          {
            className: `btn btn-sm routine-btn ${eveningDone ? 'btn-green' : 'btn-outline'}`,
            onClick: onMarkEvening,
          },
          eveningDone ? '🌙 Вечер ✓' : '🌙 Вечер'
        )
      )
    )
  );
}

js/ui/components/WeeklySparklines.js
```
import React, { useRef, useEffect, useState } from 'react';

function normalize(values, height) {
  const max = Math.max(...values, 1);
  const min = Math.min(...values, 0);
  const range = max - min || 1;
  return values.map(v => height - ((v - min) / range) * (height - 4) - 2);
}

function sparklineColor(key) {
  if (key === 'hrv') return 'var(--green)';
  if (key === 'sleep') return 'var(--blue)';
  if (key === 'strain') return 'var(--yellow)';
  return 'var(--accent)';
}

function sparklineLabel(key) {
  if (key === 'hrv') return 'HRV';
  if (key === 'sleep') return 'Сон';
  if (key === 'strain') return 'Нагрузка';
  return key;
}

function sparklineUnit(key) {
  if (key === 'hrv') return 'мс';
  if (key === 'sleep') return 'ч';
  if (key === 'strain') return '';
  return '';
}

export default function WeeklySparklines({ data }) {
  const [visible, setVisible] = useState(false);
  const prevData = useRef(data);

  useEffect(() => {
    // Animate in when data changes
    if (JSON.stringify(data) !== JSON.stringify(prevData.current)) {
      setVisible(false);
      const t = setTimeout(() => setVisible(true), 50);
      prevData.current = data;
      return () => clearTimeout(t);
    } else {
      setVisible(true);
    }
  }, [data]);

  if (!data || Object.keys(data).length === 0) return null;

  const W = 280;
  const H = 48;
  const PAD = 8;
  const gap = 6;

  return React.createElement(
    'div',
    { className: `weekly-sparklines ${visible ? 'sparklines-visible' : ''}` },
    React.createElement(
      'div',
      { className: 'sparklines-header' },
      React.createElement('span', { className: 'text-xs', style: { color: 'var(--text2)', fontWeight: 600 } }, 'Тренды за неделю')
    ),
    React.createElement(
      'div',
      { className: 'sparklines-grid' },
      Object.entries(data).map(([key, values]) => {
        if (!values || values.length === 0) return null;
        const color = sparklineColor(key);
        const points = normalize(values, H);
        const step = (W - PAD * 2) / Math.max(values.length - 1, 1);
        const pathPoints = points.map((y, i) => `${PAD + i * step},${y}`).join(' ');
        const areaPath = `M${PAD},${H} L${points.map((y, i) => `${PAD + i * step},${y}`).join(' L')} L${PAD + (values.length - 1) * step},${H} Z`;
        const lastVal = values[values.length - 1];

        return React.createElement(
          'div',
          { key, className: 'sparkline-item' },
          React.createElement(
            'div',
            { className: 'sparkline-meta' },
            React.createElement('span', { className: 'sparkline-dot', style: { backgroundColor: color } }),
            React.createElement('span', { className: 'sparkline-name' }, sparklineLabel(key)),
            React.createElement(
              'span',
              { className: 'sparkline-value', style: { color } },
              `${typeof lastVal === 'number' ? (Number.isInteger(lastVal) ? lastVal : lastVal.toFixed(1)) : lastVal}${sparklineUnit(key)}`
            )
          ),
          React.createElement(
            'svg',
            { width: W, height: H, className: 'sparkline-svg', viewBox: `0 0 ${W} ${H}` },
            // Area fill
            React.createElement('path', {
              d: areaPath,
              fill: color,
              opacity: 0.08,
            }),
            // Line
            React.createElement('polyline', {
              points: pathPoints,
              fill: 'none',
              stroke: color,
              strokeWidth: 2,
              strokeLinecap: 'round',
              strokeLinejoin: 'round',
              className: 'sparkline-path',
            }),
            // Last dot
            React.createElement('circle', {
              cx: PAD + (values.length - 1) * step,
              cy: points[points.length - 1],
              r: 3,
              fill: color,
            })
          )
        );
      })
    )
  );
}
```

js/ui/pages/TodayPage.js
```
// js/ui/pages/TodayPage.js
// Главная страница «Сегодня» — премиум UI с прогрессивным раскрытием

import React, { useContext, useState } from 'react';
import { AppStateContext, AppDispatchContext } from '../../core/AppContext.js';
import ReadinessRing from '../components/ReadinessRing.js';
import RecoveryBar from '../components/RecoveryBar.js';
import ExerciseCard from '../components/ExerciseCard.js';
import TomorrowPreview from '../components/TomorrowPreview.js';
import WeeklySparklines from '../components/WeeklySparklines.js';

/* ---------- RPE scale descriptions ---------- */
const RPE_DESCRIPTIONS = {
  0: 'Отдых — никакой активности',
  1: 'Очень легко — разминка, ходьба',
  2: 'Легко — дыхание ровное',
  3: 'Умеренно — разговаривать легко',
  4: 'Довольно тяжело — короткие фразы',
  5: 'Тяжело — дыхание частое',
  6: 'Тяжеловато — односложно говорить',
  7: 'Очень тяжело — слова с трудом',
  8: 'Крайне тяжело — невозможно говорить',
  9: 'Предельно — на грани возможностей',
  10: 'Максимум — нельзя больше',
};

function rpeZone(value) {
  if (value <= 3) return { color: 'var(--green)', label: 'Лёгкая' };
  if (value <= 6) return { color: 'var(--yellow)', label: 'Умеренная' };
  return { color: 'var(--red)', label: 'Высокая' };
}

/* ---------- main component ---------- */

export default function TodayPage() {
  const state = useContext(AppStateContext);
  const dispatch = useContext(AppDispatchContext);

  const {
    sessionPlan, trainType, readiness, autoReadiness, manualOverride,
    recoveryScore, coachAdvice, rpe, sessionNote,
    testPullUps, testPushUps, testPlank,
    trainingDone, weekLabel, tomorrowPlan, tomorrowType,
    morningDone, eveningDone, apreReasons,
    // Weekly trend data for sparklines (may be null if not computed yet)
    weeklyTrends,
  } = state;

  const {
    setRpe, setSessionNote, setTestPullUps, setTestPushUps, setTestPlank,
    handleManualOverrideChange, handleToggleTraining,
    handleMarkMorning, handleMarkEvening,
  } = dispatch;

  const isRestDay = !trainType || !sessionPlan;
  const rpeKey = Math.round(rpe);
  const rpeDesc = RPE_DESCRIPTIONS[rpeKey] || '';
  const zone = rpeZone(rpe);

  // Local state for collapsible sections
  const [showTestResults, setShowTestResults] = useState(!!sessionPlan?.isTestDay);

  return React.createElement(
    'div',
    { className: 'page-enter today-page' },

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════
    // TIER 1 — HERO: Readiness Ring
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════
    React.createElement(ReadinessRing, {
      readiness,
      autoReadiness,
      manualOverride,
      onManualOverrideChange: handleManualOverrideChange,
      recoveryScore,
    }),

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════
    // TIER 2 — Weekly Sparklines (expandable from ring)
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════
    React.createElement(WeeklySparklines, { data: weeklyTrends }),

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════
    // TIER 3 — Exercise Plan (collapsible)
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════
    React.createElement(ExerciseCard, {
      sessionPlan, trainType, weekLabel, apreReasons,
    }),

    // ── Test Results (only on test days, collapsible) ──
    sessionPlan && sessionPlan.isTestDay &&
      React.createElement(
        'div',
        { className: 'card test-results-card' },
        React.createElement(
          'div',
          { className: 'test-results-header' },
          React.createElement('span', { className: 'test-results-icon' }, '🔬'),
          React.createElement('h4', { className: 'test-results-title' }, 'Результаты тестов'),
          React.createElement(
            'button',
            {
              className: 'btn btn-sm btn-outline',
              onClick: () => setShowTestResults(v => !v),
            },
            showTestResults ? 'Свернуть' : 'Показать'
          )
        ),
        showTestResults &&
          React.createElement(
            'div',
            { className: 'test-results-grid' },
            React.createElement(
              'label',
              { className: 'test-input-label' },
              'Подтягивания',
              React.createElement('input', {
                type: 'number',
                value: testPullUps,
                onChange: e => setTestPullUps(Number(e.target.value)),
                min: 0,
              })
            ),
            React.createElement(
              'label',
              { className: 'test-input-label' },
              'Отжимания',
              React.createElement('input', {
                type: 'number',
                value: testPushUps,
                onChange: e => setTestPushUps(Number(e.target.value)),
                min: 0,
              })
            ),
            React.createElement(
              'label',
              { className: 'test-input-label' },
              'Планка (сек)',
              React.createElement('input', {
                type: 'number',
                value: testPlank,
                onChange: e => setTestPlank(Number(e.target.value)),
                min: 0,
              })
            )
          )
      ),

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════
    // RPE + Save (only on training days)
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════
    !isRestDay &&
      React.createElement(
        'div',
        { className: 'card rpe-card' },
        // RPE header
        React.createElement(
          'div',
          { className: 'rpe-card-header' },
          React.createElement('span', { className: 'rpe-card-title' }, 'Как прошла тренировка?'),
          React.createElement(
            'strong',
            { className: 'rpe-card-value', style: { color: zone.color } },
            rpe || '?'
          )
        ),
        // RPE description
        React.createElement(
          'div',
          { className: 'rpe-card-desc' },
          rpeDesc
        ),
        // RPE zone line indicator
        React.createElement(
          'div',
          { className: 'rpe-zone-line' },
          Array.from({ length: 10 }, (_, i) =>
            React.createElement('div', {
              key: i,
              className: 'rpe-zone-segment',
              style: {
                opacity: i < rpeKey ? 1 : 0.2,
                transition: 'opacity var(--transition)',
              },
            })
          )
        ),
        // RPE anchors
        React.createElement(
          'div',
          { className: 'rpe-anchors' },
          React.createElement('span', null, '0 — отдых'),
          React.createElement('span', null, '5 — тяжело'),
          React.createElement('span', null, '10 — предел')
        ),
        // Slider
        React.createElement(
          'div',
          { className: 'rpe-slider-wrap' },
          React.createElement('input', {
            type: 'range',
            min: 0,
            max: 10,
            step: 0.5,
            value: rpe,
            onChange: e => setRpe(Number(e.target.value)),
            style: { width: '100%' },
          })
        ),
        // Zone labels
        React.createElement(
          'div',
          { className: 'rpe-zone-labels' },
          React.createElement('span', null, 'лёгкая'),
          React.createElement('span', null, 'умеренная'),
          React.createElement('span', null, 'высокая')
        ),
        // Notes
        React.createElement(
          'div',
          { className: 'rpe-notes' },
          React.createElement('label', { className: 'rpe-notes-label' }, 'Заметки'),
          React.createElement('textarea', {
            value: sessionNote,
            onChange: e => setSessionNote(e.target.value),
            placeholder: 'Что получилось? Что было тяжело?',
            rows: 2,
          })
        ),
        // Save / Cancel button
        React.createElement(
          'button',
          {
            className: trainingDone ? 'btn btn-red rpe-save-btn' : 'btn btn-accent rpe-save-btn',
            onClick: handleToggleTraining,
          },
          trainingDone ? 'Отменить тренировку' : 'Сохранить тренировку'
        )
      ),

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════
    // Coach Advice
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════
    coachAdvice && coachAdvice.length > 0 &&
      React.createElement(
        'div',
        { className: 'card coach-advice-card' },
        React.createElement('h4', null, '💡 Совет тренера'),
        coachAdvice.map((tip, i) =>
          React.createElement('div', { key: i, className: 'coach-advice-item' }, tip)
        )
      ),

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════
    // Quick Stats: Tomorrow + Morning/Evening
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════
    React.createElement(TomorrowPreview, {
      tomorrowType, tomorrowPlan,
      morningDone, eveningDone,
      onMarkMorning: handleMarkMorning,
      onMarkEvening: handleMarkEvening,
    })
  );
}
```

css/styles.css
```
/* ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   css/styles.css — Персональный AI-Коуч Тренировок
   Полный редизайн: премиум-тёмная тема, анимации,
   мобильный-first, типографика
   ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

/* ── Design System ── */
:root {
  --bg: #080808;
  --surface: #111111;
  --surface2: #1a1a1a;
  --surface3: #242424;
  --surface4: #2e2e2e;
  --border: #2a2a2a;
  --border-light: #333;
  --text: #f0f0f0;
  --text2: #8a8a8a;
  --text3: #5a5a5a;

  --green: #22c55e;
  --green-bg: rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.08);
  --green-glow: rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.15);
  --yellow: #eab308;
  --yellow-bg: rgba(234, 179, 8, 0.08);
  --yellow-glow: rgba(234, 179, 8, 0.15);
  --red: #ef4444;
  --red-bg: rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.08);
  --red-glow: rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.15);
  --blue: #3b82f6;

---

## Summary of Changes

### New Components Created

1. **`ReadinessRing.js`** — Hero SVG circular progress ring (180px)
   - Animated stroke-dashoffset on load (ease-out cubic, 800ms)
   - Color-coded by readiness (green/yellow/red)
   - Center displays recovery score number (~72pt equivalent) + "Восстановление" label
   - Tappable to toggle weekly sparklines visibility
   - Readiness badge pill below ring
   - Manual override dropdown (auto/green/yellow/red)
   - Keyboard accessible (Enter/Space to toggle)

2. **`RecoveryBar.js`** — Horizontal animated progress bar
   - Animated fill on load (ease-out cubic, 600ms)
   - Color changes based on score threshold
   - Label with percentage display

3. **`ExerciseCard.js`** — Collapsible exercise plan card
   - Header with train type icon, title, exercise count
   - "Подробнее" / "Свернуть" toggle button
   - APRE reason badges always visible
   - Expanded list shows exercise name, sets×reps, notes
   - Test day styling (yellow border)

4. **`TomorrowPreview.js`** — Tomorrow's plan + routine toggles
   - Tomorrow card with type icon and exercise count
   - Morning/Evenning routine buttons with done state

5. **`WeeklySparklines.js`** — SVG sparkline charts
   - Animated line drawing (stroke-dashoffset animation)
   - Area fill under line
   - Color-coded per metric (HRV=green, sleep=blue, strain=yellow)
   - Last value dot + label
   - Fade-in transition when data changes

### TodayPage.js Restructured
- **Tier 1**: Hero ReadinessRing (large, centered, tappable)
- **Tier 2**: WeeklySparklines (expandable from ring tap)
- **Tier 3**: ExerciseCard (collapsible with "Подробнее")
- Test results card (collapsible)
- RPE card (only on training days)
- Coach advice card
- TomorrowPreview

### styles.css Additions
- `.hero-ring-container`, `.hero-ring`, `.hero-ring-svg`, `.hero-ring-bg`, `.hero-ring-fg` — Hero ring styles with drop-shadow
- `.hero-readiness-badge`, `.hero-ring-hint`, `.hero-manual-override`, `.hero-override-select` — Ring accessories
- `.weekly-sparklines`, `.sparklines-visible`, `.sparkline-item`, `.sparkline-meta`, `.sparkline-dot`, `.sparkline-name`, `.sparkline-value`, `.sparkline-svg`, `.sparkline-path` — Sparkline styles with draw animation
- `.exercise-card`, `.exercise-card-header`, `.exercise-card-icon`, `.exercise-card-info`, `.exercise-card-title`, `.exercise-card-toggle`, `.exercise-apre-badges`, `.exercise-list`, `.exercise-item`, `.exercise-item-test`, `.exercise-item-main`, `.exercise-item-name`, `.exercise-item-detail`, `.exercise-item-note` — Exercise card styles
- `.recovery-bar-wrapper`, `.recovery-bar-labels` — Recovery bar styles
- `.rpe-card`, `.rpe-card-header`, `.rpe-card-title`, `.rpe-card-value`, `.rpe-card-desc`, `.rpe-slider-wrap`, `.rpe-zone-labels`, `.rpe-notes`, `.rpe-notes-label`, `.rpe-save-btn` — RPE card styles
- `.test-results-card`, `.test-results-header`, `.test-results-icon`, `.test-results-title`, `.test-results-grid`, `.test-input-label` — Test results styles
- `.tomorrow-card`, `.tomorrow-card-inner`, `.tomorrow-icon`, `.tomorrow-label`, `.tomorrow-value` — Tomorrow card styles
- `.routine-card`, `.routine-card-title`, `.routine-buttons`, `.routine-btn` — Routine card styles
- `@keyframes fadeInUp`, `@keyframes scaleIn`, `@keyframes drawLine` — New animations
- Increased minimum touch targets to 48px throughout
- Removed old `.readiness-ring`, `.readiness-ring-bg`, `.readiness-ring-fg`, `.readiness-ring-label` (replaced by hero ring styles)
- Removed old `.exercise`, `.exercise-name`, `.exercise-detail`, `.exercise-note`, `.exercise-test` (replaced by exercise-item styles)
- Removed old `.score-display`, `.score-label` (replaced by hero ring text)

#### Fix NutritionPage.js: it uses useContext(AppStateContext) but the static array NUTRITION is not provided by the context.

ui\pages\NutritionPage.js
```
import React from 'react';
import { NUTRITION } from '../../config/constants.js';

/**
 * Страница питания.
 * @returns {JSX.Element}
 */
export default function NutritionPage() {
  return React.createElement(
    React.Fragment,
    null,
    React.createElement(
      'div',
      { className: 'card' },
      React.createElement('h2', null, 'Ежедневный ориентир питания'),
      NUTRITION.map((item, idx) =>
        React.createElement(
          'div',
          { key: idx, className: 'row', style: { marginBottom: '0.5rem' } },
          React.createElement(
            'div',
            { style: { width: '40%' } },
            React.createElement('strong', null, item.label, ':')
          ),
          React.createElement('div', { style: { width: '40%' } }, item.value),
          item.note &&
            React.createElement(
              'div',
              { style: { width: '20%', fontSize: '0.875rem', color: 'var(--text2)' } },
              item.note
            )
        )
      )
    ),
    React.createElement(
      'div',
      { className: 'card' },
      React.createElement('h2', null, 'Простой дневной план'),
      React.createElement(
        'p',
        null,
        'Завтрак: белковый (яйца, творог) + сложный углевод (овсянка) + фрукт.',
        React.createElement('br', null),
        'Обед: нежирное мясо/рыба + овощи + крупа.',
        React.createElement('br', null),
        'Ужин: лёгкий белок + овощи.',
        React.createElement('br', null),
        'Перекусы: орехи, йогурт, фрукты.',
        React.createElement('br', null),
        'Питьё: вода 2–2.5 л, ограничить кофеин после 14:00.'
      )
    )
  );
}
```
